I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[FEATURE] MCP redirects
**Is your feature request related to a problem? Please describe.**
When trying to connect to an MCP server that has been moved and is issuing a temp redirect status, the client is coded to refuse to follow the redirect. This causes the connection to fail - with no available mitigation strategy. 

**Describe the solution you'd like**
One of:
The ability to specify that the http client follows redirects in the builder.
Redirects on by default (yeah yeah breaking change)
The ability to provide my own httpclient in the builder.

**Describe alternatives you've considered**
Inherit from the StreamableHttpMcpTransport class and roll my own. I'd rather not but this is quite the roadblock for me.

**Additional context**
The issue is in dev.langchain4j.mcp.client.transport.http.StreamableHttpMcpTransport at line 163. 
The sendAsync is getting a 307 in the response status code at line 165 and it ends up down at 222 with java.lang.RuntimeException: Unexpected status code: 307. 

In my case the mcp server is working perfectly but it's been moved. 
It's not mine so I can't do anything about that. 
There's no way to set the httpClient to allow redirects and the default is NEVER.

</pr_description>

    40	public class StreamableHttpMcpTransport implements McpTransport {
    41	    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StreamableHttpMcpTransport.class);
    42	    private static final long DEFAULT_SUBSIDIARY_RETRY_MS = 5000;
    43	    private final String url;
    44	    private final McpHeadersSupplier customHeadersSupplier;
    45	    private final boolean logResponses;
    46	    private final boolean logRequests;
    47	    private final Logger trafficLog;
    48	    static final ObjectMapper OBJECT_MAPPER = new ObjectMapper();
    49	    private final AtomicReference<CompletableFuture<JsonNode>> initializeInProgress = new AtomicReference<>(null);
    50	    private volatile McpOperationHandler operationHandler;
    51	    private final HttpClient httpClient;
    52	    private final SSLContext sslContext;

    55	    private final AtomicReference<String> mcpSessionId = new AtomicReference<>();

    66	    public StreamableHttpMcpTransport(StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder builder) {
    67	        url = ensureNotNull(builder.url, "Missing server endpoint URL");
    68	        logRequests = builder.logRequests;
    69	        logResponses = builder.logResponses;
    70	        trafficLog = getOrDefault(builder.logger, McpLoggers.traffic());
    71	        Duration timeout = getOrDefault(builder.timeout, Duration.ofSeconds(60));
    72	        customHeadersSupplier = getOrDefault(builder.customHeadersSupplier, (i) -> Map.of());
    73	        sslContext = builder.sslContext;
    74	        httpVersion = builder.forceHttpVersion1_1 ? HttpClient.Version.HTTP_1_1 : HttpClient.Version.HTTP_2;
    75	        subsidiaryChannelEnabled = builder.subsidiaryChannelEnabled;
    76	        executor = getOrDefault(builder.executor, DefaultExecutorProvider.getDefaultExecutorService());
    77	        HttpClient.Builder clientBuilder =
    78	                HttpClient.newBuilder().connectTimeout(timeout).version(httpVersion);
    79	        if (builder.executor != null) {
    80	            clientBuilder.executor(builder.executor);
    81	        }
    82	        if (sslContext != null) {
    83	            clientBuilder.sslContext(sslContext);
    84	        }
    85	        httpClient = clientBuilder.build();
    86	    }

    88	    @Override
    89	    public void start(McpOperationHandler operationHandler) {
    90	        this.operationHandler = operationHandler;
    91	    }

    93	    @Override
    94	    public CompletableFuture<JsonNode> initialize(McpInitializeRequest operation) {
    95	        this.initializeRequest = operation;
    96	        CompletableFuture<JsonNode> completableFuture = execute(new McpCallContext(null, operation), false);
    97	        initializeInProgress.set(completableFuture);
    98	        return completableFuture
    99	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> {
   100	                    initializeInProgress.set(null);
   101	                    return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse);
   102	                })
   103	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> execute(
   104	                                new McpCallContext(null, new McpInitializationNotification()), false)
   105	                        .thenCompose(nullNode -> CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse)))
   106	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> {
   107	                    if (subsidiaryChannelEnabled) {
   108	                        return startSubsidiaryChannel(true)
   109	                                .thenCompose(v -> CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse));
   110	                    }
   111	                    return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse);
   112	                });
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    private HttpRequest createRequest(McpJsonRpcMessage message, McpCallContext callContext)
   116	            throws JsonProcessingException {
   117	        String body = OBJECT_MAPPER.writeValueAsString(message);
   118	        HttpRequest.BodyPublisher bodyPublisher = HttpRequest.BodyPublishers.ofString(body);
   119	        if (logRequests) {
   120	            trafficLog.info("Request: {}", body);
   121	        }
   122	        final HttpRequest.Builder builder = HttpRequest.newBuilder();
   123	        String sessionId = mcpSessionId.get();
   124	        if (sessionId != null && !(message instanceof McpInitializeRequest)) {
   125	            builder.header("Mcp-Session-Id", sessionId);
   126	        }
   127	        Map<String, String> headers = customHeadersSupplier.apply(callContext);
   128	        if (headers != null) {
   129	            headers.forEach(builder::header);
   130	        }
   131	        return builder.uri(URI.create(url))
   132	                .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
   133	                .header("Accept", "application/json,text/event-stream")
   134	                .POST(bodyPublisher)
   135	                .build();
   136	    }

   155	        execute(context, false);

   168	    private CompletableFuture<JsonNode> execute(McpCallContext context, boolean isRetry) {
   169	        Long id = context.message().getId();
   170	        if (!(context.message() instanceof McpInitializeRequest)) {
   171	            CompletableFuture<JsonNode> reinitializeInProgress = this.initializeInProgress.get();
   172	            if (reinitializeInProgress != null) {
   173	                reinitializeInProgress.join();
   174	            }
   175	        }
   176	        HttpRequest request = null;
   177	        try {
   178	            request = createRequest(
   179	                    context.message(), new McpCallContext(context.invocationContext(), context.message()));
   180	        } catch (JsonProcessingException e) {
   181	            return CompletableFuture.failedFuture(e);
   182	        }
   183	        CompletableFuture<JsonNode> future = new CompletableFuture<>();
   184	        if (id != null) {
   185	            operationHandler.startOperation(id, future);
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        httpClient
   189	                .sendAsync(request, responseInfo -> {
   190	                    if (!isExpectedStatusCode(responseInfo.statusCode())) {
   191	                        if (!(context.message() instanceof McpInitializeRequest) && responseInfo.statusCode() == 404) {
   192	                            if (!isRetry) {
   193	                                initialize(StreamableHttpMcpTransport.this.initializeRequest)
   194	                                        .thenAccept(node -> {
   195	                                            execute(context, true)
   196	                                                    .thenAccept(future::complete)
   197	                                                    .exceptionally(t -> {
   198	                                                        future.completeExceptionally(t);
   199	                                                        return null;
   200	                                                    });
   201	                                        })
   202	                                        .exceptionally(t -> {
   203	                                            future.completeExceptionally(t);
   204	                                            return null;
   205	                                        });
   206	                            }
   207	                        } else {
   208	                            future.completeExceptionally(
   209	                                    new RuntimeException("Unexpected status code: " + responseInfo.statusCode()));
   210	                        }
   211	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.discarding();
   212	                    } else {
   213	                        Optional<String> contentType = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Content-Type");
   214	                        Optional<String> mcpSessionId = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Mcp-Session-Id");
   215	                        if (mcpSessionId.isPresent()) {
   216	                            LOG.debug("Assigned MCP session ID: {}", mcpSessionId);
   217	                            StreamableHttpMcpTransport.this.mcpSessionId.set(mcpSessionId.get());
   218	                        }
   219	                        if (id != null
   220	                                && contentType.isPresent()
   221	                                && contentType.get().contains("text/event-stream")) {
   222	                            // the server has started an SSE stream
   223	                            return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.fromLineSubscriber(
   224	                                    new SseSubscriber(future, logResponses, operationHandler, trafficLog));
   225	                        } else {
   226	                            // the server has returned a regular HTTP response
   227	                            return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.mapping(
   228	                                    HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.ofString(StandardCharsets.UTF_8), responseBody -> {
   229	                                        if (logResponses) {
   230	                                            trafficLog.info("Response: {}", responseBody);
   231	                                        }
   232	                                        if (id == null) {
   233	                                            future.complete(null);
   234	                                        }
   235	                                        try {
   236	                                            JsonNode node = OBJECT_MAPPER.readTree(responseBody);
   237	                                            operationHandler.handle(node);
   238	                                            return null;
   239	                                        } catch (IOException e) {
   240	                                            future.completeExceptionally(e);
   241	                                            return null;
   242	                                        }
   243	                                    });
   244	                        }
   245	                    }
   246	                })
   247	                .exceptionally(t -> {
   248	                    future.completeExceptionally(t);
   249	                    return null;
   250	                });
   251	        return future;
   252	    }
   253	
   254	    /**
   255	     * Opens the subsidiary SSE channel by issuing an HTTP GET to the MCP endpoint.
   256	     * This allows the server to send notifications and requests to the client
   257	     * without the client first sending data via HTTP POST.
   258	     *
   259	     * @param firstAttempt if true, failures will not trigger reconnection
   260	     * @return a future that completes when the channel setup attempt finishes
   261	     */
   262	    private CompletableFuture<Void> startSubsidiaryChannel(boolean firstAttempt) {
   263	        if (closed.get()) {
   264	            return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(null);
   265	        }
   266	        HttpRequest.Builder requestBuilder = HttpRequest.newBuilder()
   267	                .uri(URI.create(url))
   268	                .header("Accept", "text/event-stream")
   269	                .GET();
   270	        String sessionId = mcpSessionId.get();
   271	        if (sessionId != null) {
   272	            requestBuilder.header("Mcp-Session-Id", sessionId);
   273	        }
   274	        String lastId = subsidiaryLastEventId.get();
   275	        if (lastId != null) {
   276	            requestBuilder.header("Last-Event-ID", lastId);
   277	        }
   278	        Map<String, String> headers = customHeadersSupplier.apply(null);
   279	        if (headers != null) {
   280	            headers.forEach(requestBuilder::header);
   281	        }
   282	        HttpRequest request = requestBuilder.build();
   283	
   284	        CompletableFuture<Void> result = new CompletableFuture<>();
   285	        SseSubscriber subscriber = new SseSubscriber(
   286	                logResponses,
   287	                operationHandler,
   288	                trafficLog,
   289	                subsidiaryLastEventId,
   290	                subsidiaryRetryMs,
   291	                this::scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect,
   292	                closed);
   293	
   294	        httpClient
   295	                .sendAsync(request, responseInfo -> {
   296	                    int statusCode = responseInfo.statusCode();
   297	                    Optional<String> contentType = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Content-Type");
   298	                    if (isExpectedStatusCode(statusCode)
   299	                            && contentType.isPresent()
   300	                            && contentType.get().contains("text/event-stream")) {
   301	                        subsidiaryChannelEstablished = true;
   302	                        LOG.debug("Subsidiary SSE channel established");
   303	                        result.complete(null);
   304	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.fromLineSubscriber(subscriber);
   305	                    } else {
   306	                        if (firstAttempt) {
   307	                            LOG.warn(
   308	                                    "Failed to open subsidiary SSE channel (status={}, contentType={}), will not re-attempt",
   309	                                    statusCode,
   310	                                    contentType.orElse("absent"));
   311	                        } else {
   312	                            LOG.debug(
   313	                                    "Failed to reconnect subsidiary SSE channel (status={}, contentType={}), scheduling retry",
   314	                                    statusCode,
   315	                                    contentType.orElse("absent"));
   316	                            if (!closed.get()) {
   317	                                scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect();
   318	                            }
   319	                        }
   320	                        result.complete(null);
   321	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.discarding();
   322	                    }
   323	                })
   324	                .exceptionally(t -> {
   325	                    if (!closed.get()) {
   326	                        if (firstAttempt) {
   327	                            LOG.warn("Failed to open subsidiary SSE channel", t);
   328	                        } else {
   329	                            LOG.debug("Subsidiary SSE channel connection failed, scheduling retry", t);
   330	                            scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect();
   331	                        }
   332	                    }
   333	                    result.complete(null);
   334	                    return null;
   335	                });
   336	        return result;
   337	    }
   338	
   339	    private void scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect() {
   340	        if (closed.get() || !subsidiaryChannelEstablished) {
   341	            return;
   342	        }
   343	        long delayMs = subsidiaryRetryMs.get();
   344	        LOG.debug("Scheduling subsidiary SSE channel reconnect in {} ms", delayMs);
   345	        Executor delayedExecutor = CompletableFuture.delayedExecutor(delayMs, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS, executor);
   346	        CompletableFuture.runAsync(
   347	                () -> {
   348	                    if (!closed.get()) {
   349	                        startSubsidiaryChannel(false);
   350	                    }
   351	                },
   352	                delayedExecutor);
   353	    }
   354	
   355	    private boolean isExpectedStatusCode(int statusCode) {
   356	        return statusCode >= 200 && statusCode < 300;
   357	    }
   358	
   359	    @Override
   360	    public void close() throws IOException {
   361	        closed.set(true);
   362	        // The httpClient.close() method only exists on JDK 21+, so invoke it only if we can.
   363	        // Replace this with a normal method call when switching the base to JDK 21+.
   364	        try {
   365	            httpClient.getClass().getMethod("close").invoke(httpClient);
   366	        } catch (NoSuchMethodException | IllegalAccessException | InvocationTargetException ignored) {
   367	        }
   368	    }

   403	        /**
   404	         * A supplier for dynamic request headers of the MCP server.

   443	            return this;

   445	
   446	        /**
   447	         * Sets a custom {@link Logger} to be used for traffic logging (both requests and responses).
   448	         * This logger will be used for both regular HTTP responses and Server-Sent Events (SSE) traffic.
   449	         * If not specified, a default logger will be used.
   450	         *
   451	         * @param logger an alternate {@link Logger} to be used instead of the default one provided by Langchain4J for traffic logging.
   452	         * @return {@code this}.
   453	         */

   455	            this.logger = logger;

   459	        /**
   460	         * An optional {@link Executor} that will be used for executing requests and handling responses.
   461	         * It will also be used for scheduling auto-reconnect attempts of the subsidiary SSE channel if that is enabled.
   462	         * If not provided, a default shared executor will be used.

   464	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder executor(Executor executor) {

   474	            this.sslContext = sslContext;

   477	
   478	        /**

   480	         */
   481	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder setHttpVersion1_1() {
   482	            this.forceHttpVersion1_1 = true;

   485	
   486	        /**
   487	         * Enables or disables the subsidiary SSE channel. When enabled, the transport
   488	         * will open an HTTP GET-based SSE stream after initialization, allowing the
   489	         * server to send notifications and requests to the client without the client
   490	         * first sending data via HTTP POST. If the server does not support the
   491	         * subsidiary channel (returns 405), the transport will log a warning and
   492	         * continue without it. If the stream breaks after being successfully
   493	         * established, the transport will automatically attempt to reconnect.
   494	         * Defaults to {@code false}.
   495	         */
   496	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder subsidiaryChannel(boolean subsidiaryChannelEnabled) {
   497	            this.subsidiaryChannelEnabled = subsidiaryChannelEnabled;
   498	            return this;
   499	        }

   502	            return new StreamableHttpMcpTransport(this);
   503	        }

    35	/**
    36	 * The legacy HTTP/SSE transport (see <a href="https://modelcontextprotocol.io/specification/2024-11-05/basic/transports#http-with-sse">specification</a>).
    37	 * Whenever possible, it is recommended to use {@link StreamableHttpMcpTransport} instead.
    38	 */
    39	@Deprecated(forRemoval = true, since = "1.4.0-beta10")
    40	public class HttpMcpTransport implements McpTransport {
    41	
    42	    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(HttpMcpTransport.class);
    43	    private final String sseUrl;
    44	    private final McpHeadersSupplier customHeadersSupplier;
    45	    private final OkHttpClient client;
    46	    private final boolean logResponses;
    47	    private final boolean logRequests;
    48	    private EventSource mcpSseEventListener;
    49	    private static final ObjectMapper OBJECT_MAPPER = new ObjectMapper();
    50	    private static final String CONTENT_TYPE = "Content-Type";
    51	    private static final String CONTENT_TYPE_JSON = "application/json";
    52	    private volatile Runnable onFailure;
    53	
    54	    // this is obtained from the server after initializing the SSE channel
    55	    private volatile String postUrl;
    56	    private volatile McpOperationHandler messageHandler;
    57	
    58	    public HttpMcpTransport(Builder builder) {
    59	        OkHttpClient.Builder httpClientBuilder = new OkHttpClient.Builder();
    60	        Duration timeout = getOrDefault(builder.timeout, Duration.ofSeconds(60));
    61	        httpClientBuilder.callTimeout(timeout);
    62	        httpClientBuilder.connectTimeout(timeout);
    63	        httpClientBuilder.readTimeout(timeout);
    64	        httpClientBuilder.writeTimeout(timeout);
    65	        this.logRequests = builder.logRequests;
    66	        if (builder.logRequests) {
    67	            httpClientBuilder.addInterceptor(new McpRequestLoggingInterceptor(builder.logger));
    68	        }
    69	        this.logResponses = builder.logResponses;
    70	        sseUrl = ensureNotNull(builder.sseUrl, "Missing SSE endpoint URL");
    71	        customHeadersSupplier = getOrDefault(builder.customHeadersSupplier, (i) -> Map.of());
    72	        client = httpClientBuilder.build();
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    @Override
    76	    public void start(McpOperationHandler messageHandler) {
    77	        this.messageHandler = messageHandler;
    78	        mcpSseEventListener = startSseChannel(logResponses);
    79	    }
    80	
    81	    @Override
    82	    public CompletableFuture<JsonNode> initialize(McpInitializeRequest operation) {
    83	        Request httpRequest = null;
    84	        Request initializationNotification = null;
    85	        try {
    86	            httpRequest = createRequest(new McpCallContext(null, operation));
    87	            initializationNotification = createRequest(new McpCallContext(null, new McpInitializationNotification()));
    88	        } catch (JsonProcessingException e) {
    89	            return CompletableFuture.failedFuture(e);
    90	        }
    91	        final Request finalInitializationNotification = initializationNotification;
    92	        return execute(httpRequest, operation.getId())
    93	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> execute(finalInitializationNotification, null)
    94	                        .thenCompose(nullNode -> CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse)));
    95	    }
    96	
    97	    @Override
    98	    public CompletableFuture<JsonNode> executeOperationWithResponse(McpClientMessage operation) {
    99	        return executeOperationWithResponse(new McpCallContext(null, operation));
   100	    }
   101	
   102	    @Override
   103	    public CompletableFuture<JsonNode> executeOperationWithResponse(McpCallContext context) {
   104	        try {
   105	            Request httpRequest = createRequest(context);
   106	            return execute(httpRequest, context.message().getId());
   107	        } catch (JsonProcessingException e) {
   108	            return CompletableFuture.failedFuture(e);
   109	        }
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    @Override
   113	    public void executeOperationWithoutResponse(McpClientMessage operation) {
   114	        executeOperationWithoutResponse(new McpCallContext(null, operation));
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    @Override
   118	    public void executeOperationWithoutResponse(McpCallContext context) {
   119	        try {
   120	            Request httpRequest = createRequest(context);
   121	            execute(httpRequest, null);
   122	        } catch (JsonProcessingException e) {
   123	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
   124	        }
   125	    }
   126	
   127	    @Override
   128	    public void checkHealth() {
   129	        // no transport-specific checks right now
   130	    }
   131	
   132	    @Override
   133	    public void onFailure(Runnable actionOnFailure) {
   134	        this.onFailure = actionOnFailure;
   135	    }
   136	
   137	    private CompletableFuture<JsonNode> execute(Request request, Long id) {
   138	        CompletableFuture<JsonNode> future = new CompletableFuture<>();
   139	        if (id != null) {
   140	            messageHandler.startOperation(id, future);
   141	        }
   142	        client.newCall(request).enqueue(new Callback() {
   143	            @Override
   144	            public void onFailure(Call call, IOException e) {
   145	                future.completeExceptionally(e);
   146	            }
   147	
   148	            @Override
   149	            public void onResponse(Call call, Response response) throws IOException {
   150	                try (response) {
   151	                    int statusCode = response.code();
   152	                    if (!isExpectedStatusCode(statusCode)) {
   153	                        future.completeExceptionally(new RuntimeException("Unexpected status code: " + statusCode));
   154	                    }
   155	                    // For messages with null ID, we don't wait for a response in the SSE channel
   156	                    if (id == null) {
   157	                        future.complete(null);
   158	                    }
   159	                }
   160	            }
   161	        });
   162	        return future;
   163	    }
   164	
   165	    private boolean isExpectedStatusCode(int statusCode) {
   166	        return statusCode >= 200 && statusCode < 300;
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    private EventSource startSseChannel(boolean logResponses) {
   170	        Request request = new Request.Builder()
   171	                .url(sseUrl)
   172	                .headers(buildCommonHeaders(null))
   173	                .build();
   174	        CompletableFuture<String> initializationFinished = new CompletableFuture<>();
   175	        SseEventListener listener =
   176	                new SseEventListener(messageHandler, logResponses, initializationFinished, onFailure);
   177	        EventSource eventSource = EventSources.createFactory(client).newEventSource(request, listener);
   178	        // wait for the SSE channel to be created, receive the POST url from the server, throw an exception if that
   179	        // failed
   180	        try {
   181	            int timeout = client.callTimeoutMillis() > 0 ? client.callTimeoutMillis() : Integer.MAX_VALUE;
   182	            String relativePostUrl = initializationFinished.get(timeout, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
   183	            postUrl = buildAbsolutePostUrl(relativePostUrl);
   184	            log.debug("Received the server's POST URL: {}", postUrl);
   185	        } catch (Exception e) {
   186	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
   187	        }
   188	        return eventSource;
   189	    }
   190	
   191	    private String buildAbsolutePostUrl(String relativePostUrl) {
   192	        try {
   193	            return URI.create(this.sseUrl).resolve(relativePostUrl).toString();
   194	        } catch (Exception e) {
   195	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
   196	        }
   197	    }
   198	
   199	    private Headers buildCommonHeaders(McpCallContext callContext) {
   200	        Headers.Builder headerBuilder = new Headers.Builder();
   201	        Map<String, String> headers = customHeadersSupplier.apply(callContext);
   202	        if (headers != null) {
   203	            headers.forEach(headerBuilder::add);
   204	        }
   205	        return headerBuilder.build();
   206	    }
   207	
   208	    private Request createRequest(McpCallContext callContext) throws JsonProcessingException {
   209	        Headers.Builder headerBuilder = new Headers.Builder().add(CONTENT_TYPE, CONTENT_TYPE_JSON);
   210	        Map<String, String> headers = customHeadersSupplier.apply(callContext);
   211	        if (headers != null) {
   212	            headers.forEach(headerBuilder::add);
   213	        }
   214	
   215	        return new Request.Builder()
   216	                .url(postUrl)
   217	                .headers(headerBuilder.build())
   218	                .post(RequestBody.create(OBJECT_MAPPER.writeValueAsBytes(callContext.message())))
   219	                .build();
   220	    }
   221	
   222	    @Override
   223	    public void close() throws IOException {
   224	        if (mcpSseEventListener != null) {
   225	            mcpSseEventListener.cancel();
   226	        }
   227	        if (client != null) {
   228	            client.dispatcher().executorService().shutdown();
   229	        }
   230	    }
   231	
   232	    public static Builder builder() {
   233	        return new Builder();
   234	    }
   235	
   236	    public static class Builder {
   237	
   238	        private String sseUrl;
   239	        private McpHeadersSupplier customHeadersSupplier;
   240	        private Duration timeout;
   241	        private boolean logRequests = false;
   242	        private boolean logResponses = false;
   243	        private Logger logger;
   244	
   245	        /**
   246	         * The initial URL where to connect to the server and request a SSE
   247	         * channel.
   248	         */
   249	        public Builder sseUrl(String sseUrl) {
   250	            this.sseUrl = sseUrl;
   251	            return this;
   252	        }
   253	
   254	        public Builder customHeaders(Map<String, String> customHeaders) {
   255	            this.customHeadersSupplier = (i) -> customHeaders;
   256	            return this;
   257	        }
   258	
   259	        public Builder customHeaders(Supplier<Map<String, String>> customHeadersSupplier) {
   260	            this.customHeadersSupplier = (i) -> customHeadersSupplier.get();
   261	            return this;
   262	        }
   263	
   264	        public Builder customHeaders(McpHeadersSupplier customMcpHeadersSupplier) {
   265	            this.customHeadersSupplier = customMcpHeadersSupplier;
   266	            return this;
   267	        }
   268	
   269	        public Builder timeout(Duration timeout) {
   270	            this.timeout = timeout;
   271	            return this;
   272	        }
   273	
   274	        public Builder logRequests(boolean logRequests) {
   275	            this.logRequests = logRequests;
   276	            return this;
   277	        }
   278	
   279	        public Builder logResponses(boolean logResponses) {
   280	            this.logResponses = logResponses;
   281	            return this;
   282	        }
   283	
   284	        /**
   285	         * @param logger an alternate {@link Logger} to be used instead of the default one provided by Langchain4J for traffic logging.
   286	         * @return {@code this}.
   287	         */
   288	        public Builder logger(Logger logger) {
   289	            this.logger = logger;
   290	            return this;
   291	        }
   292	
   293	        public HttpMcpTransport build() {
   294	            return new HttpMcpTransport(this);
   295	        }
   296	    }
   297	}

     1	package dev.langchain4j.http.client;
     2	
     3	import dev.langchain4j.exception.HttpException;
     4	import dev.langchain4j.http.client.sse.DefaultServerSentEventParser;
     5	import dev.langchain4j.http.client.sse.ServerSentEventListener;
     6	import dev.langchain4j.http.client.sse.ServerSentEventParser;
     7	
     8	/**
     9	 * A client for executing HTTP requests both synchronously and asynchronously.
    10	 * This interface is currently experimental and subject to change.
    11	 */
    12	public interface HttpClient {
    13	
    14	    /**
    15	     * Executes a given HTTP request synchronously and returns the response.
    16	     * This method blocks until the entire response is received.
    17	     *
    18	     * @param request the HTTP request to be executed.
    19	     * @return a {@link SuccessfulHttpResponse} containing the response data for successful HTTP requests (2XX status codes)
    20	     * @throws HttpException    if the server returns a client (4XX) or server (5XX) error response
    21	     * @throws RuntimeException if an unexpected error occurs during request execution (e.g., network issues, timeouts)
    22	     */
    23	    SuccessfulHttpResponse execute(HttpRequest request) throws HttpException, RuntimeException;
    24	
    25	    /**
    26	     * Executes a given HTTP request asynchronously with server-sent events (SSE) handling.
    27	     * This method returns immediately while processing continues on a separate thread.
    28	     * Events are processed through the provided {@link ServerSentEventListener}.
    29	     * <p>
    30	     * The execution flow is as follows:
    31	     * <ol>
    32	     *   <li>The request is initiated asynchronously</li>
    33	     *   <li>Received SSE data is parsed using the {@link DefaultServerSentEventParser}</li>
    34	     *   <li>Parsed events are delivered to the listener's appropriate methods</li>
    35	     *   <li>If an error occurs, {@link ServerSentEventListener#onError(Throwable)} is called</li>
    36	     * </ol>
    37	     * <p>
    38	     * If any exception is thrown from the listener's methods, the stream processing
    39	     * will be terminated and no further events will be processed.
    40	     *
    41	     * @param request  the HTTP request to be executed.
    42	     * @param listener the listener to receive parsed events and error notifications.
    43	     */
    44	    default void execute(HttpRequest request, ServerSentEventListener listener) {
    45	        execute(request, new DefaultServerSentEventParser(), listener);
    46	    }
    47	
    48	    /**
    49	     * Executes a given HTTP request asynchronously with server-sent events (SSE) handling.
    50	     * This method returns immediately while processing continues on a separate thread.
    51	     * Events are processed through the provided {@link ServerSentEventListener}.
    52	     * <p>
    53	     * The execution flow is as follows:
    54	     * <ol>
    55	     *   <li>The request is initiated asynchronously</li>
    56	     *   <li>Received SSE data is parsed using the provided parser</li>
    57	     *   <li>Parsed events are delivered to the listener's appropriate methods</li>
    58	     *   <li>If an error occurs, {@link ServerSentEventListener#onError(Throwable)} is called</li>
    59	     * </ol>
    60	     * <p>
    61	     * If any exception is thrown from the listener's methods, the stream processing
    62	     * will be terminated and no further events will be processed.
    63	     *
    64	     * @param request  the HTTP request to be executed.
    65	     * @param parser   the parser to process incoming server-sent events.
    66	     * @param listener the listener to receive parsed events and error notifications.
    67	     */
    68	    void execute(HttpRequest request, ServerSentEventParser parser, ServerSentEventListener listener);
    69	}

2026-05-30 06:04:09,350 - INFO - swea-agent-langchain4j__langchain4j-4734 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand the situation clearly. The PR description says:

1. The `StreamableHttpMcpTransport` uses `java.net.http.HttpClient` which by default has redirect policy `NEVER`.
2. When connecting to an MCP server that returns a 307 (temporary redirect), the client fails with `java.lang.RuntimeException: Unexpected status code: 307`.
3. The user wants one of:
   - Ability to specify that the HTTP client follows redirects in the builder
   - Redirects on by default
   - Ability to provide their own httpClient in the builder

The best solution is to add a `followRedirects` option in the builder (or make it default). Let me also check if the `isExpectedStatusCode` method is the right place to handle redirects, and think about the proper approach.

The `java.net.http.HttpClient` has a `followRedirects` method that can be set to:
- `HttpClient.Redirect.NEVER` (default)
- `HttpClient.Redirect.ALWAYS`
- `HttpClient.Redirect.NORMAL` (follows redirects except from HTTPS to HTTP)

The best approach is to add a builder option for `followRedirects` and default it to `NORMAL` (or `ALWAYS`). But looking at the PR description, it says "Redirects on by default (yeah yeah breaking change)" — so even the PR author acknowledges that making it default is a breaking change but acceptable.

Let me check if there are existing tests that I should look at:

import java.net.http.HttpClient;
import java.lang.reflect.Field;
import dev.langchain4j.mcp.client.transport.http.StreamableHttpMcpTransport;

public class TestRedirect {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        StreamableHttpMcpTransport transport = StreamableHttpMcpTransport.builder()
                .url("http://localhost/mcp")
                .build();
        
        Field field = StreamableHttpMcpTransport.class.getDeclaredField("httpClient");
        field.setAccessible(true);
        HttpClient httpClient = (HttpClient) field.get(transport);
        
        System.out.println("Redirect policy: " + httpClient.followRedirects());
        System.out.println("Expected: " + HttpClient.Redirect.NEVER);
        System.out.println("Match: " + (httpClient.followRedirects() == HttpClient.Redirect.NEVER));
        
        // Verify that the default is NEVER (which is the problem)
        if (httpClient.followRedirects() == HttpClient.Redirect.NEVER) {
            System.out.println("CONFIRMED: Default redirect policy is NEVER - redirects will fail!");
        }
    }
}
EOF

import sys

with open('/testbed/langchain4j-mcp/src/main/java/dev/langchain4j/mcp/client/transport/http/StreamableHttpMcpTransport.java', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

old_builder_end = """
        private boolean subsidiaryChannelEnabled = false;

        /**
         * The URL of the MCP server.
         */"""

new_builder_end = """
        private boolean subsidiaryChannelEnabled = false;
        private HttpClient.Redirect followRedirects = null;

        /**
         * The URL of the MCP server.
         */"""

content = content.replace(old_builder_end, new_builder_end)

# 2. Add the followRedirects method to the Builder class (before the build method)
old_build = """
        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport build() {
            return new StreamableHttpMcpTransport(this);
        }"""

new_build = """
        /**
         * Sets the redirect policy for the underlying HTTP client.
         * If not set, the default policy of {@link HttpClient.Redirect#NEVER} will be used.
         * Set to {@link HttpClient.Redirect#NORMAL} or {@link HttpClient.Redirect#ALWAYS}
         * to follow redirects (e.g., when the server returns a 307 Temporary Redirect).
         */
        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder followRedirects(HttpClient.Redirect followRedirects) {
            this.followRedirects = followRedirects;
            return this;
        }

        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport build() {
            return new StreamableHttpMcpTransport(this);
        }"""

content = content.replace(old_build, new_build)

# 3. Update the constructor to use the followRedirects setting
old_constructor = """        if (sslContext != null) {
            clientBuilder.sslContext(sslContext);
        }
        httpClient = clientBuilder.build();"""

new_constructor = """        if (sslContext != null) {
            clientBuilder.sslContext(sslContext);
        }
        if (builder.followRedirects != null) {
            clientBuilder.followRedirects(builder.followRedirects);
        }
        httpClient = clientBuilder.build();"""

content = content.replace(old_constructor, new_constructor)

    f.write(content)

   426	            this.timeout = timeout;
   427	            return this;

            return this;\

    68	        logRequests = builder.logRequests;
    69	        logResponses = builder.logResponses;
    70	        trafficLog = getOrDefault(builder.logger, McpLoggers.traffic());
    71	        Duration timeout = getOrDefault(builder.timeout, Duration.ofSeconds(60));
    72	        customHeadersSupplier = getOrDefault(builder.customHeadersSupplier, (i) -> Map.of());
    73	        sslContext = builder.sslContext;
    74	        httpVersion = builder.forceHttpVersion1_1 ? HttpClient.Version.HTTP_1_1 : HttpClient.Version.HTTP_2;
    75	        subsidiaryChannelEnabled = builder.subsidiaryChannelEnabled;
    76	        executor = getOrDefault(builder.executor, DefaultExecutorProvider.getDefaultExecutorService());
    77	        HttpClient.Builder clientBuilder =
    78	                HttpClient.newBuilder().connectTimeout(timeout).version(httpVersion);
    79	        if (builder.executor != null) {
    80	            clientBuilder.executor(builder.executor);
    81	        }
    82	        if (sslContext != null) {
    83	            clientBuilder.sslContext(sslContext);
    84	        }
    85	        if (builder.followRedirects != null) {
    86	            clientBuilder.followRedirects(builder.followRedirects);
    87	        }
    88	        httpClient = clientBuilder.build();
    89	    }
    90	
    91	    @Override
    92	    public void start
    93	            clientBuilder.sslContext(sslContext);
    94	        }
    95	        httpClient = clientBuilder.build();
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    @Override
    99	    public void start(McpOperationHandler operationHandler) {
   100	        this.operationHandler = operationHandler;
   101	    }
   102	
   103	    @Override
   104	    public CompletableFuture<JsonNode> initialize(McpInitializeRequest operation) {
   105	        this.initializeRequest = operation;
   106	        CompletableFuture<JsonNode> completableFuture = execute(new McpCallContext(null, operation), false);
   107	        initializeInProgress.set(completableFuture);
   108	        return completableFuture
   109	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> {
   110	                    initializeInProgress.set(null);
   111	                    return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse);
   112	                })
   113	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> execute(
   114	                                new McpCallContext(null, new McpInitializationNotification()), false)
   115	                        .thenCompose(nullNode -> CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse)))
   116	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> {
   117	                    if (subsidiaryChannelEnabled) {
   118	                        return startSubsidiaryChannel(true)
   119	                                .thenCompose(v -> CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse));
   120	                    }
   121	                    return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse);
   122	                });
   123	    }
   124	
   125	    private HttpRequest createRequest(McpJsonRpcMessage message, McpCallContext callContext)
   126	            throws JsonProcessingException {
   127	        String body = OBJECT_MAPPER.writeValueAsString(message);
   128	        HttpRequest.BodyPublisher bodyPublisher = HttpRequest.BodyPublishers.ofString(body);
   129	        if (logRequests) {
   130	            trafficLog.info("Request: {}", body);
   131	        }
   132	        final HttpRequest.Builder builder = HttpRequest.newBuilder();
   133	        String sessionId = mcpSessionId.get();
   134	        if (sessionId != null && !(message instanceof McpInitializeRequest)) {
   135	            builder.header("Mcp-Session-Id", sessionId);
   136	        }
   137	        Map<String, String> headers = customHeadersSupplier.apply(callContext);
   138	        if (headers != null) {
   139	            headers.forEach(builder::header);
   140	        }
   141	        return builder.uri(URI.create(url))
   142	                .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
   143	                .header("Accept", "application/json,text/event-stream")
   144	                .POST(bodyPublisher)
   145	                .build();
   146	    }
   147	
   148	    @Override
   149	    public CompletableFuture<JsonNode> executeOperationWithResponse(McpClientMessage operation) {
   150	        return executeOperationWithResponse(new McpCallContext(null, operation));
   151	    }
   152	
   153	    @Override
   154	    public CompletableFuture<JsonNode> executeOperationWithResponse(McpCallContext context) {
   155	        return execute(context, false);
   156	    }
   157	
   158	    @Override
   159	    public void executeOperationWithoutResponse(McpClientMessage operation) {
   160	        executeOperationWithoutResponse(new McpCallContext(null, operation));
   161	    }
   162	
   163	    @Override
   164	    public void executeOperationWithoutResponse(McpCallContext context) {
   165	        execute(context, false);
   166	    }

   169	    public void checkHealth() {
   170	        // no transport-specific checks right now
   171	    }

   174	    public void onFailure(Runnable actionOnFailure) {
   175	        this.onFailureCallback = actionOnFailure;
   176	    }
   177	
   178	    private CompletableFuture<JsonNode> execute(McpCallContext context, boolean isRetry) {
   179	        Long id = context.message().getId();
   180	        if (!(context.message() instanceof McpInitializeRequest)) {
   181	            CompletableFuture<JsonNode> reinitializeInProgress = this.initializeInProgress.get();
   182	            if (reinitializeInProgress != null) {
   183	                reinitializeInProgress.join();
   184	            }
   185	        }
   186	        HttpRequest request = null;
   187	        try {
   188	            request = createRequest(
   189	                    context.message(), new McpCallContext(context.invocationContext(), context.message()));
   190	        } catch (JsonProcessingException e) {
   191	            return CompletableFuture.failedFuture(e);
   192	        }
   193	        CompletableFuture<JsonNode> future = new CompletableFuture<>();
   194	        if (id != null) {
   195	            operationHandler.startOperation(id, future);
   196	        }
   197	
   198	        httpClient
   199	                .sendAsync(request, responseInfo -> {
   200	                    if (!isExpectedStatusCode(responseInfo.statusCode())) {
   201	                        if (!(context.message() instanceof McpInitializeRequest) && responseInfo.statusCode() == 404) {
   202	                            if (!isRetry) {
   203	                                initialize(StreamableHttpMcpTransport.this.initializeRequest)
   204	                                        .thenAccept(node -> {
   205	                                            execute(context, true)
   206	                                                    .thenAccept(future::complete)
   207	                                                    .exceptionally(t -> {
   208	                                                        future.completeExceptionally(t);
   209	                                                        return null;
   210	                                                    });
   211	                                        })
   212	                                        .exceptionally(t -> {
   213	                                            future.completeExceptionally(t);
   214	                                            return null;
   215	                                        });
   216	                            }
   217	                        } else {
   218	                            future.completeExceptionally(
   219	                                    new RuntimeException("Unexpected status code: " + responseInfo.statusCode()));
   220	                        }
   221	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.discarding();
   222	                    } else {
   223	                        Optional<String> contentType = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Content-Type");
   224	                        Optional<String> mcpSessionId = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Mcp-Session-Id");
   225	                        if (mcpSessionId.isPresent()) {
   226	                            LOG.debug("Assigned MCP session ID: {}", mcpSessionId);
   227	                            StreamableHttpMcpTransport.this.mcpSessionId.set(mcpSessionId.get());
   228	                        }
   229	                        if (id != null
   230	                                && contentType.isPresent()
   231	                                && contentType.get().contains("text/event-stream")) {
   232	                            // the server has started an SSE stream
   233	                            return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.fromLineSubscriber(
   234	                                    new SseSubscriber(future, logResponses, operationHandler, trafficLog));
   235	                        } else {
   236	                            // the server has returned a regular HTTP response
   237	                            return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.mapping(
   238	                                    HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.ofString(StandardCharsets.UTF_8), responseBody -> {
   239	                                        if (logResponses) {
   240	                                            trafficLog.info("Response: {}", responseBody);
   241	                                        }
   242	                                        if (id == null) {
   243	                                            future.complete(null);
   244	                                        }
   245	                                        try {
   246	                                            JsonNode node = OBJECT_MAPPER.readTree(responseBody);
   247	                                            operationHandler.handle(node);
   248	                                            return null;
   249	                                        } catch (IOException e) {
   250	                                            future.completeExceptionally(e);
   251	                                            return null;
   252	                                        }
   253	                                    });
   254	                        }
   255	                    }
   256	                })
   257	                .exceptionally(t -> {
   258	                    future.completeExceptionally(t);
   259	                    return null;
   260	                });
   261	        return future;
   262	    }
   263	
   264	    /**
   265	     * Opens the subsidiary SSE channel by issuing an HTTP GET to the MCP endpoint.
   266	     * This allows the server to send notifications and requests to the client
   267	     * without the client first sending data via HTTP POST.
   268	     *
   269	     * @param firstAttempt if true, failures will not trigger reconnection
   270	     * @return a future that completes when the channel setup attempt finishes
   271	     */
   272	    private CompletableFuture<Void> startSubsidiaryChannel(boolean firstAttempt) {
   273	        if (closed.get()) {
   274	            return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(null);
   275	        }
   276	        HttpRequest.Builder requestBuilder = HttpRequest.newBuilder()
   277	                .uri(URI.create(url))
   278	                .header("Accept", "text/event-stream")
   279	                .GET();
   280	        String sessionId = mcpSessionId.get();
   281	        if (sessionId != null) {
   282	            requestBuilder.header("Mcp-Session-Id", sessionId);
   283	        }
   284	        String lastId = subsidiaryLastEventId.get();
   285	        if (lastId != null) {
   286	            requestBuilder.header("Last-Event-ID", lastId);
   287	        }
   288	        Map<String, String> headers = customHeadersSupplier.apply(null);
   289	        if (headers != null) {
   290	            headers.forEach(requestBuilder::header);
   291	        }
   292	        HttpRequest request = requestBuilder.build();
   293	
   294	        CompletableFuture<Void> result = new CompletableFuture<>();
   295	        SseSubscriber subscriber = new SseSubscriber(
   296	                logResponses,
   297	                operationHandler,
   298	                trafficLog,
   299	                subsidiaryLastEventId,
   300	                subsidiaryRetryMs,
   301	                this::scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect,
   302	                closed);
   303	
   304	        httpClient
   305	                .sendAsync(request, responseInfo -> {
   306	                    int statusCode = responseInfo.statusCode();
   307	                    Optional<String> contentType = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Content-Type");
   308	                    if (isExpectedStatusCode(statusCode)
   309	                            && contentType.isPresent()
   310	                            && contentType.get().contains("text/event-stream")) {
   311	                        subsidiaryChannelEstablished = true;
   312	                        LOG.debug("Subsidiary SSE channel established");
   313	                        result.complete(null);
   314	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.fromLineSubscriber(subscriber);
   315	                    } else {
   316	                        if (firstAttempt) {
   317	                            LOG.warn(
   318	                                    "Failed to open subsidiary SSE channel (status={}, contentType={}), will not re-attempt",
   319	                                    statusCode,
   320	                                    contentType.orElse("absent"));
   321	                        } else {
   322	                            LOG.debug(
   323	                                    "Failed to reconnect subsidiary SSE channel (status={}, contentType={}), scheduling retry",
   324	                                    statusCode,
   325	                                    contentType.orElse("absent"));
   326	                            if (!closed.get()) {
   327	                                scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect();
   328	                            }
   329	                        }
   330	                        result.complete(null);
   331	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.discarding();
   332	                    }
   333	                })
   334	                .exceptionally(t -> {
   335	                    if (!closed.get()) {
   336	                        if (firstAttempt) {
   337	                            LOG.warn("Failed to open subsidiary SSE channel", t);
   338	                        } else {
   339	                            LOG.debug("Subsidiary SSE channel connection failed, scheduling retry", t);
   340	                            scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect();
   341	                        }
   342	                    }
   343	                    result.complete(null);
   344	                    return null;
   345	                });
   346	        return result;
   347	    }
   348	
   349	    private void scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect() {
   350	        if (closed.get() || !subsidiaryChannelEstablished) {
   351	            return;
   352	        }
   353	        long delayMs = subsidiaryRetryMs.get();
   354	        LOG.debug("Scheduling subsidiary SSE channel reconnect in {} ms", delayMs);
   355	        Executor delayedExecutor = CompletableFuture.delayedExecutor(delayMs, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS, executor);
   356	        CompletableFuture.runAsync(
   357	                () -> {
   358	                    if (!closed.get()) {
   359	                        startSubsidiaryChannel(false);
   360	                    }
   361	                },
   362	                delayedExecutor);
   363	    }
   364	
   365	    private boolean isExpectedStatusCode(int statusCode) {
   366	        return statusCode >= 200 && statusCode < 300;
   367	    }
   368	
   369	    @Override
   370	    public void close() throws IOException {
   371	        closed.set(true);
   372	        // The httpClient.close() method only exists on JDK 21+, so invoke it only if we can.
   373	        // Replace this with a normal method call when switching the base to JDK 21+.
   374	        try {
   375	            httpClient.getClass().getMethod("close").invoke(httpClient);
   376	        } catch (NoSuchMethodException | IllegalAccessException | InvocationTargetException ignored) {
   377	        }
   378	    }

   421	        }

   424	         * A supplier for dynamic request headers of the MCP server.
   425	         * The supplier is called for each request, allowing headers to be updated dynamically.
   426	         */
   427	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder customHeaders(McpHeadersSupplier customHeadersSupplier) {
   428	            this.customHeadersSupplier = customHeadersSupplier;
   429	            return this;
   430	        }
   431	
   432	        /**

   434	         * timeouts are handled by the MCP client itself.

   436	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder timeout(Duration timeout) {
   437	            this.timeout = timeout;
   438	            return this;
   439	        }
   440

   443	         */

   445	            this.logRequests = logRequests;
   446	            return this;
   447	        }

   451	         */

   453	            this.logResponses = logResponses;
   454	            return this;
   455	        }
   456	
   457	        /**
   458	         * Sets a custom {@link Logger} to be used for traffic logging (both requests and responses).
   459	         * This logger will be used for both regular HTTP responses and Server-Sent Events (SSE) traffic.
   460	         * If not specified, a default logger will be used.
   461	         *
   462	         * @param logger an alternate {@link Logger} to be used instead of the default one provided by Langchain4J for traffic logging.
   463	         * @return {@code this}.
   464	         */
   465	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder logger(Logger logger) {
   466	            this.logger = logger;
   467	            return this;
   468	        }
   469	
   470	        /**
   471	         * An optional {@link Executor} that will be used for executing requests and handling responses.
   472	         * It will also be used for scheduling auto-reconnect attempts of the subsidiary SSE channel if that is enabled.
   473	         * If not provided, a default shared executor will be used.
   474	         */
   475	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder executor(Executor executor) {
   476	            this.executor = executor;
   477	            return this;
   478	        }

   482	         * allowing private CAs or certificates.

   485	            this.sslContext = sslContext;
   486	            return this;
   487	        }

   491	         */
   492	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder setHttpVersion1_1() {
   493	            this.forceHttpVersion1_1 = true;
   494	            return this;
   495	        }
   496	
   497	        /**
   498	         * Enables or disables the subsidiary SSE channel. When enabled, the transport
   499	         * will open an HTTP GET-based SSE stream after initialization, allowing the
   500	         * server to send notifications and requests to the client without the client
   501	         * first sending data via HTTP POST. If the server does not support the
   502	         * subsidiary channel (returns 405), the transport will log a warning and
   503	         * continue without it. If the stream breaks after being successfully
   504	         * established, the transport will automatically attempt to reconnect.
   505	         * Defaults to {@code false}.
   506	         */
   507	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder subsidiaryChannel(boolean subsidiaryChannelEnabled) {
   508	            this.subsidiaryChannelEnabled = subsidiaryChannelEnabled;

   510	        }
   511

   513	         * Sets the redirect policy for the underlying HTTP client.
   514	         * If not set, the default policy of {@link HttpClient.Redirect#NEVER} will be used.
   515	         * Set to {@link HttpClient.Redirect#NORMAL} or {@link HttpClient.Redirect#ALWAYS}
   516	         * to follow redirects (e.g., when the server returns a 307 Temporary Redirect).
   517	         */
   518	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder followRedirects(HttpClient.Redirect followRedirects) {
   519	            this.followRedirects = followRedirects;
   520	            return this;
   521	        }

   524	            return new StreamableHttpMcpTransport(this);
   525	        }

    40	public class StreamableHttpMcpTransport implements McpTransport {
    41	    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StreamableHttpMcpTransport.class);
    42	    private static final long DEFAULT_SUBSIDIARY_RETRY_MS = 5000;
    43	    private final String url;
    44	    private final McpHeadersSupplier customHeadersSupplier;
    45	    private final boolean logResponses;
    46	    private final boolean logRequests;
    47	    private final Logger trafficLog;
    48	    static final ObjectMapper OBJECT_MAPPER = new ObjectMapper();
    49	    private final AtomicReference<CompletableFuture<JsonNode>> initializeInProgress = new AtomicReference<>(null);
    50	    private volatile McpOperationHandler operationHandler;
    51	    private final HttpClient httpClient;
    52	    private final SSLContext sslContext;
    53	    private final HttpClient.Version httpVersion;
    54	    private McpInitializeRequest initializeRequest;
    55	    private final AtomicReference<String> mcpSessionId = new AtomicReference<>();
    56	
    57	    // Subsidiary SSE channel fields
    58	    private final boolean subsidiaryChannelEnabled;
    59	    private volatile Runnable onFailureCallback;
    60	    private volatile boolean subsidiaryChannelEstablished;
    61	    private final AtomicReference<String> subsidiaryLastEventId = new AtomicReference<>();
    62	    private final AtomicLong subsidiaryRetryMs = new AtomicLong(DEFAULT_SUBSIDIARY_RETRY_MS);
    63	    private final Executor executor;

    66	    public StreamableHttpMcpTransport(StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder builder) {
    67	        url = ensureNotNull(builder.url, "Missing server endpoint URL");
    68	        logRequests = builder.logRequests;
    69	        logResponses = builder.logResponses;
    70	        trafficLog = getOrDefault(builder.logger, McpLoggers.traffic());
    71	        Duration timeout = getOrDefault(builder.timeout, Duration.ofSeconds(60));
    72	        customHeadersSupplier = getOrDefault(builder.customHeadersSupplier, (i) -> Map.of());
    73	        sslContext = builder.sslContext;
    74	        httpVersion = builder.forceHttpVersion1_1 ? HttpClient.Version.HTTP_1_1 : HttpClient.Version.HTTP_2;
    75	        subsidiaryChannelEnabled = builder.subsidiaryChannelEnabled;
    76	        executor = getOrDefault(builder.executor, DefaultExecutorProvider.getDefaultExecutorService());
    77	        HttpClient.Builder clientBuilder =
    78	                HttpClient.newBuilder().connectTimeout(timeout).version(httpVersion);
    79	        if (builder.executor != null) {
    80	            clientBuilder.executor(builder.executor);
    81	        }
    82	        if (sslContext != null) {
    83	            clientBuilder.sslContext(sslContext);
    84	        }
    85	        httpClient = clientBuilder.build();
    86	    }

    88	    @Override
    89	    public void start(McpOperationHandler operationHandler) {
    90	        this.operationHandler = operationHandler;
    91	    }

    93	    @Override
    94	    public CompletableFuture<JsonNode> initialize(McpInitializeRequest operation) {
    95	        this.initializeRequest = operation;
    96	        CompletableFuture<JsonNode> completableFuture = execute(new McpCallContext(null, operation), false);
    97	        initializeInProgress.set(completableFuture);
    98	        return completableFuture
    99	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> {
   100	                    initializeInProgress.set(null);
   101	                    return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse);
   102	                })
   103	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> execute(
   104	                                new McpCallContext(null, new McpInitializationNotification()), false)
   105	                        .thenCompose(nullNode -> CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse)))
   106	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> {
   107	                    if (subsidiaryChannelEnabled) {
   108	                        return startSubsidiaryChannel(true)
   109	                                .thenCompose(v -> CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse));
   110	                    }
   111	                    return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse);
   112	                });
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    private HttpRequest createRequest(McpJsonRpcMessage message, McpCallContext callContext)
   116	            throws JsonProcessingException {
   117	        String body = OBJECT_MAPPER.writeValueAsString(message);
   118	        HttpRequest.BodyPublisher bodyPublisher = HttpRequest.BodyPublishers.ofString(body);
   119	        if (logRequests) {
   120	            trafficLog.info("Request: {}", body);
   121	        }
   122	        final HttpRequest.Builder builder = HttpRequest.newBuilder();
   123	        String sessionId = mcpSessionId.get();
   124	        if (sessionId != null && !(message instanceof McpInitializeRequest)) {
   125	            builder.header("Mcp-Session-Id", sessionId);
   126	        }
   127	        Map<String, String> headers = customHeadersSupplier.apply(callContext);
   128	        if (headers != null) {
   129	            headers.forEach(builder::header);
   130	        }
   131	        return builder.uri(URI.create(url))
   132	                .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
   133	                .header("Accept", "application/json,text/event-stream")
   134	                .POST(bodyPublisher)
   135	                .build();
   136	    }

   140	        return executeOperationWithResponse(new McpCallContext(null, operation));
   141	    }

   151	    }

   154	    public void executeOperationWithoutResponse(McpCallContext context) {
   155	        execute(context, false);
   156	    }

   160	        // no transport-specific checks right now

   165	        this.onFailureCallback = actionOnFailure;

   168	    private CompletableFuture<JsonNode> execute(McpCallContext context, boolean isRetry) {
   169	        Long id = context.message().getId();
   170	        if (!(context.message() instanceof McpInitializeRequest)) {
   171	            CompletableFuture<JsonNode> reinitializeInProgress = this.initializeInProgress.get();
   172	            if (reinitializeInProgress != null) {
   173	                reinitializeInProgress.join();
   174	            }
   175	        }
   176	        HttpRequest request = null;
   177	        try {
   178	            request = createRequest(
   179	                    context.message(), new McpCallContext(context.invocationContext(), context.message()));
   180	        } catch (JsonProcessingException e) {
   181	            return CompletableFuture.failedFuture(e);
   182	        }
   183	        CompletableFuture<JsonNode> future = new CompletableFuture<>();
   184	        if (id != null) {
   185	            operationHandler.startOperation(id, future);
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        httpClient
   189	                .sendAsync(request, responseInfo -> {
   190	                    if (!isExpectedStatusCode(responseInfo.statusCode())) {
   191	                        if (!(context.message() instanceof McpInitializeRequest) && responseInfo.statusCode() == 404) {
   192	                            if (!isRetry) {
   193	                                initialize(StreamableHttpMcpTransport.this.initializeRequest)
   194	                                        .thenAccept(node -> {
   195	                                            execute(context, true)
   196	                                                    .thenAccept(future::complete)
   197	                                                    .exceptionally(t -> {
   198	                                                        future.completeExceptionally(t);
   199	                                                        return null;
   200	                                                    });
   201	                                        })
   202	                                        .exceptionally(t -> {
   203	                                            future.completeExceptionally(t);
   204	                                            return null;
   205	                                        });
   206	                            }
   207	                        } else {
   208	                            future.completeExceptionally(
   209	                                    new RuntimeException("Unexpected status code: " + responseInfo.statusCode()));
   210	                        }
   211	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.discarding();
   212	                    } else {
   213	                        Optional<String> contentType = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Content-Type");
   214	                        Optional<String> mcpSessionId = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Mcp-Session-Id");
   215	                        if (mcpSessionId.isPresent()) {
   216	                            LOG.debug("Assigned MCP session ID: {}", mcpSessionId);
   217	                            StreamableHttpMcpTransport.this.mcpSessionId.set(mcpSessionId.get());
   218	                        }
   219	                        if (id != null
   220	                                && contentType.isPresent()
   221	                                && contentType.get().contains("text/event-stream")) {
   222	                            // the server has started an SSE stream
   223	                            return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.fromLineSubscriber(
   224	                                    new SseSubscriber(future, logResponses, operationHandler, trafficLog));
   225	                        } else {
   226	                            // the server has returned a regular HTTP response
   227	                            return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.mapping(
   228	                                    HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.ofString(StandardCharsets.UTF_8), responseBody -> {
   229	                                        if (logResponses) {
   230	                                            trafficLog.info("Response: {}", responseBody);
   231	                                        }
   232	                                        if (id == null) {
   233	                                            future.complete(null);
   234	                                        }
   235	                                        try {
   236	                                            JsonNode node = OBJECT_MAPPER.readTree(responseBody);
   237	                                            operationHandler.handle(node);
   238	                                            return null;
   239	                                        } catch (IOException e) {
   240	                                            future.completeExceptionally(e);
   241	                                            return null;
   242	                                        }
   243	                                    });
   244	                        }
   245	                    }
   246	                })
   247	                .exceptionally(t -> {
   248	                    future.completeExceptionally(t);
   249	                    return null;
   250	                });
   251	        return future;
   252	    }
   253	
   254	    /**
   255	     * Opens the subsidiary SSE channel by issuing an HTTP GET to the MCP endpoint.
   256	     * This allows the server to send notifications and requests to the client
   257	     * without the client first sending data via HTTP POST.
   258	     *
   259	     * @param firstAttempt if true, failures will not trigger reconnection
   260	     * @return a future that completes when the channel setup attempt finishes
   261	     */
   262	    private CompletableFuture<Void> startSubsidiaryChannel(boolean firstAttempt) {
   263	        if (closed.get()) {
   264	            return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(null);
   265	        }
   266	        HttpRequest.Builder requestBuilder = HttpRequest.newBuilder()
   267	                .uri(URI.create(url))
   268	                .header("Accept", "text/event-stream")
   269	                .GET();
   270	        String sessionId = mcpSessionId.get();
   271	        if (sessionId != null) {
   272	            requestBuilder.header("Mcp-Session-Id", sessionId);
   273	        }
   274	        String lastId = subsidiaryLastEventId.get();
   275	        if (lastId != null) {
   276	            requestBuilder.header("Last-Event-ID", lastId);
   277	        }
   278	        Map<String, String> headers = customHeadersSupplier.apply(null);
   279	        if (headers != null) {
   280	            headers.forEach(requestBuilder::header);
   281	        }
   282	        HttpRequest request = requestBuilder.build();
   283	
   284	        CompletableFuture<Void> result = new CompletableFuture<>();
   285	        SseSubscriber subscriber = new SseSubscriber(
   286	                logResponses,
   287	                operationHandler,
   288	                trafficLog,
   289	                subsidiaryLastEventId,
   290	                subsidiaryRetryMs,
   291	                this::scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect,
   292	                closed);
   293	
   294	        httpClient
   295	                .sendAsync(request, responseInfo -> {
   296	                    int statusCode = responseInfo.statusCode();
   297	                    Optional<String> contentType = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Content-Type");
   298	                    if (isExpectedStatusCode(statusCode)
   299	                            && contentType.isPresent()
   300	                            && contentType.get().contains("text/event-stream")) {
   301	                        subsidiaryChannelEstablished = true;
   302	                        LOG.debug("Subsidiary SSE channel established");
   303	                        result.complete(null);
   304	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.fromLineSubscriber(subscriber);
   305	                    } else {
   306	                        if (firstAttempt) {
   307	                            LOG.warn(
   308	                                    "Failed to open subsidiary SSE channel (status={}, contentType={}), will not re-attempt",
   309	                                    statusCode,
   310	                                    contentType.orElse("absent"));
   311	                        } else {
   312	                            LOG.debug(
   313	                                    "Failed to reconnect subsidiary SSE channel (status={}, contentType={}), scheduling retry",
   314	                                    statusCode,
   315	                                    contentType.orElse("absent"));
   316	                            if (!closed.get()) {
   317	                                scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect();
   318	                            }
   319	                        }
   320	                        result.complete(null);
   321	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.discarding();
   322	                    }
   323	                })
   324	                .exceptionally(t -> {
   325	                    if (!closed.get()) {
   326	                        if (firstAttempt) {
   327	                            LOG.warn("Failed to open subsidiary SSE channel", t);
   328	                        } else {
   329	                            LOG.debug("Subsidiary SSE channel connection failed, scheduling retry", t);
   330	                            scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect();
   331	                        }
   332	                    }
   333	                    result.complete(null);
   334	                    return null;
   335	                });
   336	        return result;
   337	    }
   338	
   339	    private void scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect() {
   340	        if (closed.get() || !subsidiaryChannelEstablished) {
   341	            return;
   342	        }
   343	        long delayMs = subsidiaryRetryMs.get();
   344	        LOG.debug("Scheduling subsidiary SSE channel reconnect in {} ms", delayMs);
   345	        Executor delayedExecutor = CompletableFuture.delayedExecutor(delayMs, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS, executor);
   346	        CompletableFuture.runAsync(
   347	                () -> {
   348	                    if (!closed.get()) {
   349	                        startSubsidiaryChannel(false);
   350	                    }
   351	                },
   352	                delayedExecutor);
   353	    }
   354	
   355	    private boolean isExpectedStatusCode(int statusCode) {
   356	        return statusCode >= 200 && statusCode < 300;
   357	    }
   358	
   359	    @Override
   360	    public void close() throws IOException {
   361	        closed.set(true);
   362	        // The httpClient.close() method only exists on JDK 21+, so invoke it only if we can.
   363	        // Replace this with a normal method call when switching the base to JDK 21+.
   364	        try {
   365	            httpClient.getClass().getMethod("close").invoke(httpClient);
   366	        } catch (NoSuchMethodException | IllegalAccessException | InvocationTargetException ignored) {
   367	        }
   368	    }

   371	        return new Builder();

   391	            this.url = url;
   392	            return this;

   395	        /**
   396	         * The request headers of the MCP server.
