   398	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder customHeaders(Map<String, String> customHeaders) {
   399	            this.customHeadersSupplier = (i) -> customHeaders;
   400	            return this;
   401	        }
   402	
   403	        /**
   404	         * A supplier for dynamic request headers of the MCP server.
   405	         * The supplier is called for each request, allowing headers to be updated dynamically.
   406	         */
   407	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder customHeaders(Supplier<Map<String, String>> customHeadersSupplier) {
   408	            this.customHeadersSupplier = i -> customHeadersSupplier.get();
   409	            return this;
   410	        }
   411	
   412	        /**
   413	         * A supplier for dynamic request headers of the MCP server.
   414	         * The supplier is called for each request, allowing headers to be updated dynamically.
   415	         */
   416	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder customHeaders(McpHeadersSupplier customHeadersSupplier) {
   417	            this.customHeadersSupplier = customHeadersSupplier;
   418	            return this;
   419	        }
   420	
   421	        /**
   422	         * The connection timeout (applied on the http client level). Application-level
   423	         * timeouts are handled by the MCP client itself.

   425	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder timeout(Duration timeout) {
   426	            this.timeout = timeout;
   427	            return this;
   428	        }

   435	            return this;

   442	            this.logResponses = logResponses;
   443	            return this;
   444	        }
   445	
   446	        /**
   447	         * Sets a custom {@link Logger} to be used for traffic logging (both requests and responses).
   448	         * This logger will be used for both regular HTTP responses and Server-Sent Events (SSE) traffic.
   449	         * If not specified, a default logger will be used.
   450	         *
   451	         * @param logger an alternate {@link Logger} to be used instead of the default one provided by Langchain4J for traffic logging.
   452	         * @return {@code this}.
   453	         */
   454	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder logger(Logger logger) {
   455	            this.logger = logger;
   456	            return this;
   457	        }

   459	        /**
   460	         * An optional {@link Executor} that will be used for executing requests and handling responses.
   461	         * It will also be used for scheduling auto-reconnect attempts of the subsidiary SSE channel if that is enabled.
   462	         * If not provided, a default shared executor will be used.
   463	         */
   464	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder executor(Executor executor) {
   465	            this.executor = executor;
   466	            return this;
   467	        }

   471	         * allowing private CAs or certificates.

   473	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder sslContext(SSLContext sslContext) {
   474	            this.sslContext = sslContext;
   475	            return this;
   476	        }
   477	
   478	        /**

   480	         */
   481	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder setHttpVersion1_1() {
   482	            this.forceHttpVersion1_1 = true;
   483	            return this;
   484	        }
   485	
   486	        /**
   487	         * Enables or disables the subsidiary SSE channel. When enabled, the transport
   488	         * will open an HTTP GET-based SSE stream after initialization, allowing the
   489	         * server to send notifications and requests to the client without the client
   490	         * first sending data via HTTP POST. If the server does not support the
   491	         * subsidiary channel (returns 405), the transport will log a warning and
   492	         * continue without it. If the stream breaks after being successfully
   493	         * established, the transport will automatically attempt to reconnect.
   494	         * Defaults to {@code false}.
   495	         */
   496	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder subsidiaryChannel(boolean subsidiaryChannelEnabled) {
   497	            this.subsidiaryChannelEnabled = subsidiaryChannelEnabled;
   498	            return this;
   499	        }

   502	            return new StreamableHttpMcpTransport(this);
   503	        }

    40	public class StreamableHttpMcpTransport implements McpTransport {
    41	    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StreamableHttpMcpTransport.class);
    42	    private static final long DEFAULT_SUBSIDIARY_RETRY_MS = 5000;
    43	    private final String url;

    48	    static final ObjectMapper OBJECT_MAPPER = new ObjectMapper();
    49	    private final AtomicReference<CompletableFuture<JsonNode>> initializeInProgress = new AtomicReference<>(null);
    50	    private volatile McpOperationHandler operationHandler;
    51	    private final HttpClient httpClient;
    52	    private final SSLContext sslContext;

    66	    public StreamableHttpMcpTransport(StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder builder) {
    67	        url = ensureNotNull(builder.url, "Missing server endpoint URL");
    68	        logRequests = builder.logRequests;
    69	        logResponses = builder.logResponses;
    70	        trafficLog = getOrDefault(builder.logger, McpLoggers.traffic());
    71	        Duration timeout = getOrDefault(builder.timeout, Duration.ofSeconds(60));
    72	        customHeadersSupplier = getOrDefault(builder.customHeadersSupplier, (i) -> Map.of());
    73	        sslContext = builder.sslContext;
    74	        httpVersion = builder.forceHttpVersion1_1 ? HttpClient.Version.HTTP_1_1 : HttpClient.Version.HTTP_2;
    75	        subsidiaryChannelEnabled = builder.subsidiaryChannelEnabled;
    76	        executor = getOrDefault(builder.executor, DefaultExecutorProvider.getDefaultExecutorService());
    77	        HttpClient.Builder clientBuilder =
    78	                HttpClient.newBuilder().connectTimeout(timeout).version(httpVersion);
    79	        if (builder.executor != null) {
    80	            clientBuilder.executor(builder.executor);
    81	        }
    82	        if (sslContext != null) {
    83	            clientBuilder.sslContext(sslContext);
    84	        }
    85	        if (builder.followRedirects != null) {
    86	            clientBuilder.followRedirects(builder.followRedirects);
    87	        }
    88	        httpClient = clientBuilder.build();
    89	    }

    91	    @Override
    92	    public void start(McpOperationHandler operationHandler) {
    93	        this.operationHandler = operationHandler;
    94	    }
    95	
    96	    @Override
    97	    public CompletableFuture<JsonNode> initialize(McpInitializeRequest operation) {
    98	        this.initializeRequest = operation;
    99	        CompletableFuture<JsonNode> completableFuture = execute(new McpCallContext(null, operation), false);
   100	        initializeInProgress.set(completableFuture);
   101	        return completableFuture
   102	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> {
   103	                    initializeInProgress.set(null);
   104	                    return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse);
   105	                })
   106	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> execute(
   107	                                new McpCallContext(null, new McpInitializationNotification()), false)
   108	                        .thenCompose(nullNode -> CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse)))
   109	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> {
   110	                    if (subsidiaryChannelEnabled) {
   111	                        return startSubsidiaryChannel(true)
   112	                                .thenCompose(v -> CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse));
   113	                    }
   114	                    return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse);
   115	                });
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    private HttpRequest createRequest(McpJsonRpcMessage message, McpCallContext callContext)
   119	            throws JsonProcessingException {
   120	        String body = OBJECT_MAPPER.writeValueAsString(message);
   121	        HttpRequest.BodyPublisher bodyPublisher = HttpRequest.BodyPublishers.ofString(body);
   122	        if (logRequests) {
   123	            trafficLog.info("Request: {}", body);
   124	        }
   125	        final HttpRequest.Builder builder = HttpRequest.newBuilder();
   126	        String sessionId = mcpSessionId.get();
   127	        if (sessionId != null && !(message instanceof McpInitializeRequest)) {
   128	            builder.header("Mcp-Session-Id", sessionId);
   129	        }
   130	        Map<String, String> headers = customHeadersSupplier.apply(callContext);
   131	        if (headers != null) {
   132	            headers.forEach(builder::header);
   133	        }
   134	        return builder.uri(URI.create(url))
   135	                .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
   136	                .header("Accept", "application/json,text/event-stream")
   137	                .POST(bodyPublisher)
   138	                .build();
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    @Override
   142	    public CompletableFuture<JsonNode> executeOperationWithResponse(McpClientMessage operation) {
   143	        return executeOperationWithResponse(new McpCallContext(null, operation));
   144	    }
   145	
   146	    @Override
   147	    public CompletableFuture<JsonNode> executeOperationWithResponse(McpCallContext context) {
   148	        return execute(context, false);
   149	    }
   150	
   151	    @Override
   152	    public void executeOperationWithoutResponse(McpClientMessage operation) {
   153	        executeOperationWithoutResponse(new McpCallContext(null, operation));
   154	    }
   155	
   156	    @Override
   157	    public void executeOperationWithoutResponse(McpCallContext context) {
   158	        execute(context, false);
   159	    }

   163	        // no transport-specific checks right now
   164	    }

   167	    public void onFailure(Runnable actionOnFailure) {
   168	        this.onFailureCallback = actionOnFailure;

   170	
   171	    private CompletableFuture<JsonNode> execute(McpCallContext context, boolean isRetry) {
   172	        Long id = context.message().getId();
   173	        if (!(context.message() instanceof McpInitializeRequest)) {
   174	            CompletableFuture<JsonNode> reinitializeInProgress = this.initializeInProgress.get();
   175	            if (reinitializeInProgress != null) {
   176	                reinitializeInProgress.join();
   177	            }
   178	        }
   179	        HttpRequest request = null;
   180	        try {
   181	            request = createRequest(
   182	                    context.message(), new McpCallContext(context.invocationContext(), context.message()));
   183	        } catch (JsonProcessingException e) {
   184	            return CompletableFuture.failedFuture(e);
   185	        }
   186	        CompletableFuture<JsonNode> future = new CompletableFuture<>();
   187	        if (id != null) {
   188	            operationHandler.startOperation(id, future);
   189	        }
   190	
   191	        httpClient
   192	                .sendAsync(request, responseInfo -> {
   193	                    if (!isExpectedStatusCode(responseInfo.statusCode())) {
   194	                        if (!(context.message() instanceof McpInitializeRequest) && responseInfo.statusCode() == 404) {
   195	                            if (!isRetry) {
   196	                                initialize(StreamableHttpMcpTransport.this.initializeRequest)
   197	                                        .thenAccept(node -> {
   198	                                            execute(context, true)
   199	                                                    .thenAccept(future::complete)
   200	                                                    .exceptionally(t -> {
   201	                                                        future.completeExceptionally(t);
   202	                                                        return null;
   203	                                                    });
   204	                                        })
   205	                                        .exceptionally(t -> {
   206	                                            future.completeExceptionally(t);
   207	                                            return null;
   208	                                        });
   209	                            }
   210	                        } else {
   211	                            future.completeExceptionally(
   212	                                    new RuntimeException("Unexpected status code: " + responseInfo.statusCode()));
   213	                        }
   214	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.discarding();
   215	                    } else {
   216	                        Optional<String> contentType = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Content-Type");
   217	                        Optional<String> mcpSessionId = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Mcp-Session-Id");
   218	                        if (mcpSessionId.isPresent()) {
   219	                            LOG.debug("Assigned MCP session ID: {}", mcpSessionId);
   220	                            StreamableHttpMcpTransport.this.mcpSessionId.set(mcpSessionId.get());
   221	                        }
   222	                        if (id != null
   223	                                && contentType.isPresent()
   224	                                && contentType.get().contains("text/event-stream")) {
   225	                            // the server has started an SSE stream
   226	                            return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.fromLineSubscriber(
   227	                                    new SseSubscriber(future, logResponses, operationHandler, trafficLog));
   228	                        } else {
   229	                            // the server has returned a regular HTTP response
   230	                            return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.mapping(
   231	                                    HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.ofString(StandardCharsets.UTF_8), responseBody -> {
   232	                                        if (logResponses) {
   233	                                            trafficLog.info("Response: {}", responseBody);
   234	                                        }
   235	                                        if (id == null) {
   236	                                            future.complete(null);
   237	                                        }
   238	                                        try {
   239	                                            JsonNode node = OBJECT_MAPPER.readTree(responseBody);
   240	                                            operationHandler.handle(node);
   241	                                            return null;
   242	                                        } catch (IOException e) {
   243	                                            future.completeExceptionally(e);
   244	                                            return null;
   245	                                        }
   246	                                    });
   247	                        }
   248	                    }
   249	                })
   250	                .exceptionally(t -> {
   251	                    future.completeExceptionally(t);
   252	                    return null;
   253	                });
   254	        return future;
   255	    }
   256	
   257	    /**
   258	     * Opens the subsidiary SSE channel by issuing an HTTP GET to the MCP endpoint.
   259	     * This allows the server to send notifications and requests to the client
   260	     * without the client first sending data via HTTP POST.
   261	     *
   262	     * @param firstAttempt if true, failures will not trigger reconnection
   263	     * @return a future that completes when the channel setup attempt finishes
   264	     */
   265	    private CompletableFuture<Void> startSubsidiaryChannel(boolean firstAttempt) {
   266	        if (closed.get()) {
   267	            return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(null);
   268	        }
   269	        HttpRequest.Builder requestBuilder = HttpRequest.newBuilder()
   270	                .uri(URI.create(url))
   271	                .header("Accept", "text/event-stream")
   272	                .GET();
   273	        String sessionId = mcpSessionId.get();
   274	        if (sessionId != null) {
   275	            requestBuilder.header("Mcp-Session-Id", sessionId);
   276	        }
   277	        String lastId = subsidiaryLastEventId.get();
   278	        if (lastId != null) {
   279	            requestBuilder.header("Last-Event-ID", lastId);
   280	        }
   281	        Map<String, String> headers = customHeadersSupplier.apply(null);
   282	        if (headers != null) {
   283	            headers.forEach(requestBuilder::header);
   284	        }
   285	        HttpRequest request = requestBuilder.build();
   286	
   287	        CompletableFuture<Void> result = new CompletableFuture<>();
   288	        SseSubscriber subscriber = new SseSubscriber(
   289	                logResponses,
   290	                operationHandler,
   291	                trafficLog,
   292	                subsidiaryLastEventId,
   293	                subsidiaryRetryMs,
   294	                this::scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect,
   295	                closed);
   296	
   297	        httpClient
   298	                .sendAsync(request, responseInfo -> {
   299	                    int statusCode = responseInfo.statusCode();
   300	                    Optional<String> contentType = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Content-Type");
   301	                    if (isExpectedStatusCode(statusCode)
   302	                            && contentType.isPresent()
   303	                            && contentType.get().contains("text/event-stream")) {
   304	                        subsidiaryChannelEstablished = true;
   305	                        LOG.debug("Subsidiary SSE channel established");
   306	                        result.complete(null);
   307	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.fromLineSubscriber(subscriber);
   308	                    } else {
   309	                        if (firstAttempt) {
   310	                            LOG.warn(
   311	                                    "Failed to open subsidiary SSE channel (status={}, contentType={}), will not re-attempt",
   312	                                    statusCode,
   313	                                    contentType.orElse("absent"));
   314	                        } else {
   315	                            LOG.debug(
   316	                                    "Failed to reconnect subsidiary SSE channel (status={}, contentType={}), scheduling retry",
   317	                                    statusCode,
   318	                                    contentType.orElse("absent"));
   319	                            if (!closed.get()) {
   320	                                scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect();
   321	                            }
   322	                        }
   323	                        result.complete(null);
   324	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.discarding();
   325	                    }
   326	                })
   327	                .exceptionally(t -> {
   328	                    if (!closed.get()) {
   329	                        if (firstAttempt) {
   330	                            LOG.warn("Failed to open subsidiary SSE channel", t);
   331	                        } else {
   332	                            LOG.debug("Subsidiary SSE channel connection failed, scheduling retry", t);
   333	                            scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect();
   334	                        }
   335	                    }
   336	                    result.complete(null);
   337	                    return null;
   338	                });
   339	        return result;
   340	    }
   341	
   342	    private void scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect() {
   343	        if (closed.get() || !subsidiaryChannelEstablished) {
   344	            return;
   345	        }
   346	        long delayMs = subsidiaryRetryMs.get();
   347	        LOG.debug("Scheduling subsidiary SSE channel reconnect in {} ms", delayMs);
   348	        Executor delayedExecutor = CompletableFuture.delayedExecutor(delayMs, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS, executor);
   349	        CompletableFuture.runAsync(
   350	                () -> {
   351	                    if (!closed.get()) {
   352	                        startSubsidiaryChannel(false);
   353	                    }
   354	                },
   355	                delayedExecutor);
   356	    }
   357	
   358	    private boolean isExpectedStatusCode(int statusCode) {
   359	        return statusCode >= 200 && statusCode < 300;
   360	    }
   361	
   362	    @Override
   363	    public void close() throws IOException {
   364	        closed.set(true);
   365	        // The httpClient.close() method only exists on JDK 21+, so invoke it only if we can.
   366	        // Replace this with a normal method call when switching the base to JDK 21+.
   367	        try {
   368	            httpClient.getClass().getMethod("close").invoke(httpClient);
   369	        } catch (NoSuchMethodException | IllegalAccessException | InvocationTargetException ignored) {
   370	        }
   371	    }
   372	
   373	    public static Builder builder() {
   374	        return new Builder();
   375	    }
   376	
   377	    public static class Builder {
   378	
   379	        private Executor executor;
   380	        private String url;
   381	        private McpHeadersSupplier customHeadersSupplier;
   382	        private Duration timeout;
   383	        private boolean logRequests = false;
   384	        private boolean logResponses = false;
   385	        private Logger logger;
   386	        private SSLContext sslContext;
   387	        private boolean forceHttpVersion1_1;
   388	        private boolean subsidiaryChannelEnabled = false;
   389	        private HttpClient.Redirect followRedirects = null;
   390	
   391	        /**
   392	         * The URL of the MCP server.
   393	         */
   394	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder url(String url) {
   395	            this.url = url;
   396	            return this;
   397	        }
   398	
   399	        /**
   400	         * The request headers of the MCP server.
   401	         */
   402	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder customHeaders(Map<String, String> customHeaders) {
   403	            this.customHeadersSupplier = (i) -> customHeaders;
   404	            return this;
   405	        }
   406	
   407	        /**
   408	         * A supplier for dynamic request headers of the MCP server.
   409	         * The supplier is called for each request, allowing headers to be updated dynamically.
   410	         */
   411	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder customHeaders(Supplier<Map<String, String>> customHeadersSupplier) {
   412	            this.customHeadersSupplier = i -> customHeadersSupplier.get();
   413	            return this;
   414	        }
   415	
   416	        /**
   417	         * A supplier for dynamic request headers of the MCP server.
   418	         * The supplier is called for each request, allowing headers to be updated dynamically.
   419	         */
   420	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder customHeaders(McpHeadersSupplier customHeadersSupplier) {
   421	            this.customHeadersSupplier = customHeadersSupplier;
   422	            return this;
   423	        }
   424	
   425	        /**
   426	         * The connection timeout (applied on the http client level). Application-level
   427	         * timeouts are handled by the MCP client itself.
   428	         */
   429	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder timeout(Duration timeout) {
   430	            this.timeout = timeout;
   431	            return this;
   432	        }
   433	
   434	        /**
   435	         * Whether to log all requests that are sent over this transport.
   436	         */
   437	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder logRequests(boolean logRequests) {
   438	            this.logRequests = logRequests;
   439	            return this;
   440	        }
   441	
   442	        /**
   443	         * Whether to log all responses received over this transport.
   444	         */
   445	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder logResponses(boolean logResponses) {
   446	            this.logResponses = logResponses;
   447	            return this;
   448	        }
   449	
   450	        /**
   451	         * Sets a custom {@link Logger} to be used for traffic logging (both requests and responses).
   452	         * This logger will be used for both regular HTTP responses and Server-Sent Events (SSE) traffic.
   453	         * If not specified, a default logger will be used.
   454	         *
   455	         * @param logger an alternate {@link Logger} to be used instead of the default one provided by Langchain4J for traffic logging.
   456	         * @return {@code this}.
   457	         */
   458	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder logger(Logger logger) {
   459	            this.logger = logger;
   460	            return this;
   461	        }
   462	
   463	        /**
   464	         * An optional {@link Executor} that will be used for executing requests and handling responses.
   465	         * It will also be used for scheduling auto-reconnect attempts of the subsidiary SSE channel if that is enabled.
   466	         * If not provided, a default shared executor will be used.
   467	         */
   468	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder executor(Executor executor) {
   469	            this.executor = executor;
   470	            return this;
   471	        }
   472	
   473	        /**
   474	         * Supplies a custom {@link SSLContext} used when establishing HTTPS connections to the MCP server,
   475	         * allowing private CAs or certificates.
   476	         */
   477	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder sslContext(SSLContext sslContext) {
   478	            this.sslContext = sslContext;
   479	            return this;
   480	        }
   481	
   482	        /**
   483	         * Forces the transport to use HTTP/1.1 instead of the default HTTP/2.
   484	         */
   485	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder setHttpVersion1_1() {
   486	            this.forceHttpVersion1_1 = true;
   487	            return this;
   488	        }
   489	
   490	        /**
   491	         * Enables or disables the subsidiary SSE channel. When enabled, the transport
   492	         * will open an HTTP GET-based SSE stream after initialization, allowing the
   493	         * server to send notifications and requests to the client without the client
   494	         * first sending data via HTTP POST. If the server does not support the
   495	         * subsidiary channel (returns 405), the transport will log a warning and
   496	         * continue without it. If the stream breaks after being successfully
   497	         * established, the transport will automatically attempt to reconnect.
   498	         * Defaults to {@code false}.
   499	         */
   500	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder subsidiaryChannel(boolean subsidiaryChannelEnabled) {
   501	            this.subsidiaryChannelEnabled = subsidiaryChannelEnabled;
   502	            return this;
   503	        }
   504	
   505	        /**
   506	         * Sets the redirect policy for the underlying HTTP client.
   507	         * If not set, the default policy of {@link HttpClient.Redirect#NEVER} will be used.
   508	         * Set to {@link HttpClient.Redirect#NORMAL} or {@link HttpClient.Redirect#ALWAYS}
   509	         * to follow redirects (e.g., when the server returns a 307 Temporary Redirect).
   510	         * @param followRedirects the redirect policy to use
   511	         * @return {@code this}
   512	         */
   513	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder followRedirects(HttpClient.Redirect followRedirects) {
   514	            this.followRedirects = followRedirects;
   515	            return this;
   516	        }
   517	
   518	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport build() {
   519	            return new StreamableHttpMcpTransport(this);
   520	        }
   521	    }
   522	}

import java.net.http.HttpClient;
import java.lang.reflect.Field;
import dev.langchain4j.mcp.client.transport.http.StreamableHttpMcpTransport;

public class TestRedirect2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        // Test 1: Default (no followRedirects set) - should keep NEVER
        StreamableHttpMcpTransport transport1 = StreamableHttpMcpTransport.builder()
                .url("http://localhost/mcp")
                .build();
        
        Field field = StreamableHttpMcpTransport.class.getDeclaredField("httpClient");
        field.setAccessible(true);
        HttpClient httpClient1 = (HttpClient) field.get(transport1);
        
        System.out.println("Test 1 - Default: " + httpClient1.followRedirects());
        if (httpClient1.followRedirects() == HttpClient.Redirect.NEVER) {
            System.out.println("  PASS: Default is NEVER (backward compatible)");
        } else {
            System.out.println("  FAIL: Expected NEVER but got " + httpClient1.followRedirects());
        }
        
        // Test 2: Set NORMAL redirect policy
        StreamableHttpMcpTransport transport2 = StreamableHttpMcpTransport.builder()
                .url("http://localhost/mcp")
                .followRedirects(HttpClient.Redirect.NORMAL)
                .build();
        
        HttpClient httpClient2 = (HttpClient) field.get(transport2);
        
        System.out.println("Test 2 - NORMAL: " + httpClient2.followRedirects());
        if (httpClient2.followRedirects() == HttpClient.Redirect.NORMAL) {
            System.out.println("  PASS: NORMAL redirect policy set correctly");
        } else {
            System.out.println("  FAIL: Expected NORMAL but got " + httpClient2.followRedirects());
        }
        
        // Test 3: Set ALWAYS redirect policy
        StreamableHttpMcpTransport transport3 = StreamableHttpMcpTransport.builder()
                .url("http://localhost/mcp")
                .followRedirects(HttpClient.Redirect.ALWAYS)
                .build();
        
        HttpClient httpClient3 = (HttpClient) field.get(transport3);
        
        System.out.println("Test 3 - ALWAYS: " + httpClient3.followRedirects());
        if (httpClient3.followRedirects() == HttpClient.Redirect.ALWAYS) {
            System.out.println("  PASS: ALWAYS redirect policy set correctly");
        } else {
            System.out.println("  FAIL: Expected ALWAYS but got " + httpClient3.followRedirects());
        }
        
        System.out.println("\nAll tests completed!");
    }
}

1. **Backward compatible**: The default behavior remains `NEVER` (no redirect following), so existing code won't break.
2. **New `followRedirects` builder method**: Users can now set the redirect policy to `NORMAL` or `ALWAYS` to follow redirects like 307 (Temporary Redirect).
3. **Flexible**: Users can choose the exact redirect policy they need.

Let me also think about edge cases:

1. **What if someone sets `null`?** The code checks `if (builder.followRedirects != null)` before applying, so setting null explicitly (or not setting it at all) just keeps the default `NEVER` behavior.

2. **What about the subsidiary channel (SSE)?** The same `httpClient` is used for both regular requests and the subsidiary SSE channel, so redirects would be followed for both. This is correct behavior.

3. **What about `HttpMcpTransport`?** That's the legacy deprecated transport using OkHttp. The PR description specifically mentions `StreamableHttpMcpTransport`, so I've focused on that. The OkHttp-based transport could potentially have similar issues, but it's deprecated for removal.

The implementation looks complete. Let me run all the MCP tests to make sure nothing is broken:







🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && ./mvnw test -pl langchain4j-mcp -am -o -Dtest="StreamableHttpMcpTransportTest,HttpMcpTransportTest" -Dsurefire.failIfNoSpecifiedTests=false 2>&1 | tail -30
